                    <script id="scr_5kIDcw8g1hPEhfKSEjP1r5p-noclrbt" nonce="16EU1F75I6yc7F+euV5+mA==">
                     try {
                            const formId = '5kIDcw8g1hPEhfKSEjP1r5';
                            const panelIndex = 'p-noclrbt';
                            const panelWrap = `[data-pnl='${panelIndex}']`;
                            const isUS = window.optimizely && (window.optimizely.get('visitor').location !== undefined)
                              && window.optimizely.get('visitor').location.country === 'US';
                            // const form = document.getElementById('5kIDcw8g1hPEhfKSEjP1r5');
                            const form = $(`${panelWrap} #${formId}`);
                            fetch('/workers/hbs/partials/formFields/5kIDcw8g1hPEhfKSEjP1r5?getGlobal=true&formType=rollouts-form&lang=en-US')
                              .then(res => res.json())
                              .then((res) => {
                                const isClearbit = 'false';
                                const formType = 'rollouts-form';
                                const scriptTag = document.getElementById(`scr_5kIDcw8g1hPEhfKSEjP1r5${panelIndex}`);
                  
                                if (((formType === 'signup-form' || formType === 'rollouts-form') && res.signup) || formType !== 'signup-form') {
                                  if (scriptTag.parentElement !== null) scriptTag.parentElement.innerHTML = res.html;
                                  $(`${panelWrap} .form-wrapper`).attr('style', 'display: grid');
                  
                                  const formWrapper = `${panelWrap} .multistep .form-wrapper`;
                                  if (isClearbit === 'true' && isUS !== undefined && res.user === undefined) {
                                    $(formWrapper).clone().addClass('step-2').insertAfter($(formWrapper));
                                    $(`${formWrapper}:not(.step-2)`).addClass('step-1 active');
                                    const $step1 = $(`${formWrapper}.step-1`);
                                    const $step2 = $(`${formWrapper}.step-2`);
                                    $step1.find('.field:not(:first-child)').remove();
                  
                                    const $field = form.find('field');
                                    $field.addClass('email');
                  
                                    $step1.find('.field input').attr('data-parsley-group', 'block-0');
                                    if (formType === 'contact-sales-form') {
                                      $step2.find('.field.reason').appendTo($step1);
                                      $step1.find('.field.reason select').attr('data-parsley-group', 'block-0');
                                    }
                                    $step1.show();
                                    //$step1.style.display = 'grid';
                                    $step2.find('.field:first-child').remove();
                                    $step2.find('.field input').attr('data-parsley-group', 'block-1');
                                    $step2.find('.field select').attr('data-parsley-group', 'block-1');
                                    $(`${panelWrap} button[type=submit]`).clone().insertAfter(`${panelWrap} button[type=submit]`)
                                      .attr({type: 'button', id: `next-btn-${formId}`, 'data-button-text': 'Next'}).addClass('next').text('Next');
                                    $(`${panelWrap} button[type=submit]`).addClass('submit').prop('disabled', true).hide();
                                    $(`${panelWrap} #${formId}`).append('<p class="form-steps mt-2 txt-c">Step <span>1</span> of 2</p>');
                                  } else {
                                    $(`${panelWrap} .form-wrapper`).attr('style', 'display: grid');
                                  }
                                  if (res.mkto && res.user) {
                                    $(`${panelWrap} .prog-prof-intro`).show();
                                    $(`${panelWrap} .prog-prof-intro span b`).text(`, ${res.user}!`);
                                  }
                                  if (res.terms) {
                                    $(`${panelWrap} .terms loaded div`).html(res.terms);
                                    $(`${panelWrap} .terms loaded`).show();
                                  }
                                  const countryField = $('select[name="country"]');
                                  if (countryField) countryField.on('change', (e) => window.countrySelect(e));
                                } else {
                                  $(`.form-wrapper`).attr('style', 'display: grid');
                                }
                              })
                              .catch(function (err) {
                                $(`.form-wrapper`).attr('style', 'display: grid');
                                console.log(err);
                              });
                          } catch (error) {
                            console.log(error);

                 <form class="new-form-builder demandbase-form contact-sales-form" data-mktoid="2543" data-next-content-type="panelHeadlineSummaryCta" data-next-panel="7lB2zBMhrtrI8xMJZBqasW" data-optimizely-form-type="contact-sales-form" data-parsley-required-message="Required" data-parsley-validate="" data-slug="homepage-redesign" id="4l5wneOO8jVXZyY6hlJjqd" method="POST">

                  <div class="form-wrapper m-t-2 txt-l" style="display: none">
                   <script id="scr_4l5wneOO8jVXZyY6hlJjqdp-noclrbt" nonce="16EU1F75I6yc7F+euV5+mA==">
                    try {
                                  const formId = '4l5wneOO8jVXZyY6hlJjqd';
                                  const panelIndex = 'p-noclrbt';
                                  const panelWrap = `[data-pnl='${panelIndex}']`;
                                  const isUS = window.optimizely && (window.optimizely.get('visitor').location !== undefined)
                                    && window.optimizely.get('visitor').location.country === 'US';
                                  // const form = document.getElementById('4l5wneOO8jVXZyY6hlJjqd');
                                  const form = $(`${panelWrap} #${formId}`);
                                  fetch('/workers/hbs/partials/formFields/4l5wneOO8jVXZyY6hlJjqd?getGlobal=true&formType=contact-sales-form&lang=en-US')
                                    .then(res => res.json())
                                    .then((res) => {
                                      const isClearbit = 'false';
                                      const formType = 'contact-sales-form';
                                      const scriptTag = document.getElementById(`scr_4l5wneOO8jVXZyY6hlJjqd${panelIndex}`);
                        
                                      if (((formType === 'signup-form' || formType === 'rollouts-form') && res.signup) || formType !== 'signup-form') {
                                        if (scriptTag.parentElement !== null) scriptTag.parentElement.innerHTML = res.html;
                                        $(`${panelWrap} .form-wrapper`).attr('style', 'display: grid');
                        
                                        const formWrapper = `${panelWrap} .multistep .form-wrapper`;
                                        if (isClearbit === 'true' && isUS !== undefined && res.user === undefined) {
                                          $(formWrapper).clone().addClass('step-2').insertAfter($(formWrapper));
                                          $(`${formWrapper}:not(.step-2)`).addClass('step-1 active');
                                          const $step1 = $(`${formWrapper}.step-1`);
                                          const $step2 = $(`${formWrapper}.step-2`);
                                          $step1.find('.field:not(:first-child)').remove();
                        
                                          const $field = form.find('field');
                                          $field.addClass('email');
                        
                                          $step1.find('.field input').attr('data-parsley-group', 'block-0');
                                          if (formType === 'contact-sales-form') {
                                            $step2.find('.field.reason').appendTo($step1);
                                            $step1.find('.field.reason select').attr('data-parsley-group', 'block-0');
                                          }
                                          $step1.show();
                                          //$step1.style.display = 'grid';
                                          $step2.find('.field:first-child').remove();
                                          $step2.find('.field input').attr('data-parsley-group', 'block-1');
                                          $step2.find('.field select').attr('data-parsley-group', 'block-1');
                                          $(`${panelWrap} button[type=submit]`).clone().insertAfter(`${panelWrap} button[type=submit]`)
                                            .attr({type: 'button', id: `next-btn-${formId}`, 'data-button-text': 'Next'}).addClass('next').text('Next');
                                          $(`${panelWrap} button[type=submit]`).addClass('submit').prop('disabled', true).hide();
                                          $(`${panelWrap} #${formId}`).append('<p class="form-steps mt-2 txt-c">Step <span>1</span> of 2</p>');
                                        } else {
                                          $(`${panelWrap} .form-wrapper`).attr('style', 'display: grid');
                                        }
                                        if (res.mkto && res.user) {
                                          $(`${panelWrap} .prog-prof-intro`).show();
                                          $(`${panelWrap} .prog-prof-intro span b`).text(`, ${res.user}!`);
                                        }
                                        if (res.terms) {
                                          $(`${panelWrap} .terms loaded div`).html(res.terms);
                                          $(`${panelWrap} .terms loaded`).show();
                                        }
                                        const countryField = $('select[name="country"]');
                                        if (countryField) countryField.on('change', (e) => window.countrySelect(e));
                                      } else {
                                        $(`.form-wrapper`).attr('style', 'display: grid');
                                      }
                                    })
                                    .catch(function (err) {
                                      $(`.form-wrapper`).attr('style', 'display: grid');
                                      console.log(err);
                                    });
                                } catch (error) {
                                  console.log(error);
                                }

                                    && window.optimizely.get('visitor').location.country === 'US';
                                  // const form = document.getElementById('5kIDcw8g1hPEhfKSEjP1r5');
                                  const form = $(`${panelWrap} #${formId}`);
                                  fetch('/workers/hbs/partials/formFields/5kIDcw8g1hPEhfKSEjP1r5?getGlobal=true&formType=rollouts-form&lang=en-US')
                                    .then(res => res.json())
                                    .then((res) => {
                                      const isClearbit = 'false';
                                      const formType = 'rollouts-form';
                                      const scriptTag = document.getElementById(`scr_5kIDcw8g1hPEhfKSEjP1r5${panelIndex}`);
                        
                                      if (((formType === 'signup-form' || formType === 'rollouts-form') && res.signup) || formType !== 'signup-form') {
                                        if (scriptTag.parentElement !== null) scriptTag.parentElement.innerHTML = res.html;
                                        $(`${panelWrap} .form-wrapper`).attr('style', 'display: grid');
                        
                                        const formWrapper = `${panelWrap} .multistep .form-wrapper`;
                                        if (isClearbit === 'true' && isUS !== undefined && res.user === undefined) {
                                          $(formWrapper).clone().addClass('step-2').insertAfter($(formWrapper));
                                          $(`${formWrapper}:not(.step-2)`).addClass('step-1 active');
                                          const $step1 = $(`${formWrapper}.step-1`);
                                          const $step2 = $(`${formWrapper}.step-2`);
                                          $step1.find('.field:not(:first-child)').remove();
                        
                                          const $field = form.find('field');
                                          $field.addClass('email');
                        
                                          $step1.find('.field input').attr('data-parsley-group', 'block-0');
                                          if (formType === 'contact-sales-form') {
                                            $step2.find('.field.reason').appendTo($step1);
                                            $step1.find('.field.reason select').attr('data-parsley-group', 'block-0');
                                          }
                                          $step1.show();
                                          //$step1.style.display = 'grid';
                                          $step2.find('.field:first-child').remove();
                                          $step2.find('.field input').attr('data-parsley-group', 'block-1');

                                          $(`${panelWrap} button[type=submit]`).clone().insertAfter(`${panelWrap} button[type=submit]`)
